The Truth About the Suicide of a Beautiful Woman at the Hua'an Hotel 147

Chen Sufen Commits Suicide Out of Deep Affection

Deng Ruiren's False Promises Lead to Tragedy

According to the Xin Xin News Agency, the suicide of Cantonese woman Chen Sufen by poisoning in room 412 on the fourth floor of the Hua'an Building on Jing'an Temple Road on the morning of April 16th has attracted considerable attention. When reporters began investigating, they read the woman's diary at the Xinzha Police Station and copied excerpts, which were published in various newspapers on April 17th, as readers are probably aware. At that time, calls were made to the people involved at the Baolong Hospital on Baike Road, and to Yu Zhibo, who arranged for the collection and burial after the court's inspection. Due to the urgency of the situation, details were vague. Subsequently, after reporters investigated from various sources and followed the clues in the woman's diary, the truth became clear. It is now being reported again, hoping it will be welcomed by readers and not seen as yesterday's news.

Chen Sufen, the Female Lead, Was a Famous Courtesan in Guangdong Province. 148

Sufen's name is a recent change; her name in the courtesan registry was Leng Hong. She was beautiful and refined. She attended school in her youth, but due to poverty, she was sold into prostitution at the age of fifteen. Her mother died early, and she only had an elderly father, now sixty years old. Chen was proud and unwilling to associate with the corrupt, so although she was sought after by many wealthy and powerful men, she did not favor any of them, as she was unwilling to commit herself for life. She also called herself "Tears of the Cliff" to express her ambition to choose someone to serve and escape the sea of ​​suffering. Chen never forgot this for a single day. She met

Deng Ruiren, the Male Lead, is Currently 149

Deng Ruiren, is currently the Chairman of the Board of Directors of the Guohua Bank of Shanghai and the owner of the Cangzhou Hotel. He was the Director of Finance of the 19th Route Army during the January 28th Incident in Shanghai. He is wealthy and handsome, and a well-known figure in the financial circles of Shanghai and Guangdong. He admired Chen's reputation for a long time and eventually met her at a social event. He was immediately smitten, and from then on, he was devoted to her. Chen, seeing that Deng was associated with high-ranking officials and dignitaries, and that he had both fame and fortune, was unconsciously moved. Chen then committed herself to him, and they promised to marry each other.

The Result of Deng and Chen's Relationship: 150

However, Deng already had a wife at home and was also known for being strict. Therefore, although he swore to Chen that they would fly together, it was difficult to fulfill his promise. Deng then spent some money on Chen, hoping to settle this case, but Chen insisted on her original intention and refused to marry anyone but Deng, vowing to remain single for life. Therefore, the two sides remained undecided for a long time. This was in 1923. In 1924, Sufen was just eighteen years old and gave birth to a daughter in Guangdong, who is now named "Xiangling." The birth of this child can be said to have stirred up the stagnant well, rekindling the dying embers. Chen also took this opportunity to reiterate her old promise to Deng. At this time, Deng was truly in a dilemma. If he agreed, it would be impossible, but if he abandoned her, it would be unrighteous. He had no choice but to make false promises and temporarily build a golden house. However, Chen was completely infatuated and was not satisfied until a formal wedding was held, so she constantly urged him.

She Went to Hangzhou to Study for a Few Years. But, Good Things Never Come Easy, 151

Just as Chen Sufen had found a place to settle down and was waiting for good news, she suddenly noticed that Deng's visits became infrequent and that she might not receive any more money. She tried every means to meet him, but to no avail. Even when they exchanged letters, they were like stones sinking into the sea. Recently, Deng came to Shanghai on a mission and lived in a villa. Chen found out and followed him from Guangdong to Shanghai by ship. After many efforts, she finally met Chen, and their negotiations almost went to extremes. Later, Deng, fearing that it would affect his mission, asked Chen to go to Hangzhou to study for a few years and then talk about marriage, promising to do his best to support her. Chen, feeling helpless, packed her bags and went to Hangzhou, and arranged for Deng to visit her in a day or two.

The Circumstances of Staying at Hua'an: After Chen Arrived in Hangzhou, she Lived 152

at the YMCA. Deng was forced to go to Hangzhou due to the pressure of the situation. At that time, Sufen thought that Deng's visit would show his passion for her and that he would be affectionate towards her. But again, things did not go as planned. Deng arranged to meet Chen on a boat, but later, fearing that there would be too many eyes and ears and that it would damage his reputation, he broke the appointment. Chen was resentful and strongly criticized Deng, fearing that he would abandon her altogether. At the same time, the YMCA in Hangzhou had heard rumors, so Chen resolutely left Hangzhou with Deng to Shanghai, forcing him to fulfill his previous promise. Deng kept making excuses, and finally, through the mediation of Deng's friend, Deng agreed to fulfill the promise a month later and rented room 412 in Hua'an Building for Chen to live in, telling her to wait patiently. This is how Chen Sufen came to live in Hua'an Building.

A Final Night of Intimacy and Farewell: After Sufen Moved to Hua'an, 153

Deng would occasionally find time to visit her. On the night before Chen's suicide (the 15th), Deng secretly went to Hua'an at around 11:00 PM. Chen had just gone out, so he left immediately. He went again at 12:00 AM, and Chen had already gone to bed. The two were very intimate. Later, during their conversation, they talked about marriage again. Deng's words inevitably revealed some signs of prevarication. Chen then said that she would commit suicide to show Deng her determination and to prove that she had not let him down. Deng continued to perfunctorily comfort her. Unexpectedly, Chen ran into the bathroom, grabbed a bottle of Lysol used for bathing, pulled out the wooden stopper, and poured it straight into her mouth. Deng was unable to rescue her and, fearing that the incident would be discovered and be detrimental to him, he quickly put on his clothes and ran out, borrowing a phone nearby to call for a doctor. He then rushed to a friend's house and asked him to come forward and handle the matter. This is the reason for the strange phone call to Baolong Hospital and Yu Zhibo's arrangement for the coffin and burial.

Sister Rui is Deng Ruiren: The above is what the reporter 154

obtained after many days of private visits and secret inquiries. At the same time, because the woman's life was pitiful, fearing that outsiders might not know the details, it is specially reported. As for the diary entry on March 2, which mentions "Sister Rui, do you know how foolish someone is in love with you in this world?" This "Sister Rui" is Deng Ruiren. The woman feared that her diary might be lost and implicate Deng, so she wrote in a female persona to avoid suspicion. From this, it can be seen that Sufen's love for Deng can be described as meticulous, and her intentions can be described as sincere. At the same time, because of her infatuation, fearing that Deng would change his mind, she even prayed to God: "I once asked for a divination in Hangzhou, asking about how my relationship with Sister Rui will end up." This is clear evidence.

Many Shadows in the Diary: The most important entry in the diary 155

is that of March 26th. The diary also ends on this date, as

at this time, Sufen had just arrived in Shanghai from Guangdong and had just found Deng's whereabouts, but their meeting had no results. Therefore, the entry on March 26th is full of complaints. As a result, her words were careless and revealed her true feelings. For the sake of the readers' exploration, it is copied below without being verbose: "So, I call him from now on, but he doesn't listen. I write to him, but he doesn't read it. I can only tear it up and throw it into the wastebasket. But he treats me like this, and I don't resent him. The more he hates me, the more my guilt is reduced. I only hope that it will not affect the feelings of him and his wife. No matter how painful I am, I am willing to endure it." "The reason why I was eager to leave the YMCA this time was also to preserve his reputation, and also because Mr. Long guaranteed that I could live here." "Also, the people in charge of the YMCA know that there have been two or three phone calls to Shanghai looking for me, and they often say that a relative lives in Shanghai. If they investigate, they will definitely know the relationship between Sister Rui and me. Wouldn't that affect his position? At the same time, he and his wife will definitely have a tragedy because of me." "My usual love, especially this time with Rui, I have never announced it to anyone. I always suppressed it in my heart." "This time I really died in Shanghai, and no one can understand my heart. In short, good people are not allowed to live in this society. If I were willing to be a degenerate person, I would not have failed so much." "I will keep all the promises he made to me." "Before I met him, I could casually marry someone, but after this time and this intoxication with him, how can I marry someone else?" "The most unforgettable thing is the two nights on the boat and the month in Hua'an. When he came to Hangzhou to see me before leaving Shanghai this time, the impression of the three nights after eating cold rice will not be erased even at the time of death." "Now I hate it, but after that month in Hua'an was over, I should have died immediately, that would have been the most courageous thing to do, but what I hate the most is that this evil daughter is dragging me down. If it weren't for her, I would have died long ago, without waiting to live until now and suffer this pain." "But the most pitiful thing is that my X (Xiangling) is innocently suffering. Committing all kinds of sins, it is also my X (Sufen) and his (Rui)'s love child X (Rui) is a past life's karma, that's right. My father is already over sixty years old and will eventually come to an end. If I anger him to death this time, it will save him from suffering in this dirty society. People will eventually die, it cannot be avoided, but the most pitiful thing is X (Xiangling), who is now ten years old. When will she be able to get through these decades of suffering? Thinking of this, I can't wait to run back to Guangdong, hold my daughter, and jump into the sea together to die."

A Major Murder Case: Looking at this woman's relationship with Deng, 156

it can be said that she was the most infatuated. Deng, on the other hand, only provided assistance when absolutely necessary. The power of money is truly great. Tenants in the French Concession Demand 159

Rent Conversion from Tael to Yuan, Zhou Lianji Returns the Original Letter, Tenants Continue to Protest

The tenants along the streets of the French Concession, including Balijiao Road, West Zilaihuo Street, Caishi Street, and Yuqing Lane, have jointly written to the landlord Zhou Lianji and a certain accounting firm, requesting permission to change the rent from taels to yuan (originally calculated in silver taels) to alleviate the burden due to the recent economic downturn and poor business. After sending the letter, the landlord Zhou Lianji returned the original document, but marked on the back of the envelope, "This property is handled by the accounting firm." The accounting firm also replied to the tenants, stating that they should request the landlord. Because the tenants did not achieve their goal of changing the rent, they gathered all the tenants along the street yesterday afternoon to discuss relief methods. They all said that when the French Concession's economy had not yet declined last year, the tenants in the lane requested a rent reduction, and the landlord and tenant representatives negotiated in May, approving the reduction. Only our tenants along the street did not receive any rights, which is obviously unfair. Moreover, the current economic downturn is at its extreme. If no measures are taken to provide relief, there is a real fear that bankruptcies will follow one another. Therefore, it was decided to appoint Tan Huisheng of Yonghua Company, Jin Hongxun of Guohua Company, Hong Yongyu of Brothers Socks Factory, Zhang Huiqiao of Meifeng Silk Store, Shen Yongkang of Yongkang Sauce Garden, Gu Guangfu of Xieji Egg Shop, Yao Zhaoji of Chunjiang Hotel, Jiang Maotang of Ruyi Restaurant, and Wang Yongkang of Xiekangsheng as authorized representatives to continue negotiations with the landlord Zhou Lianji and a certain accounting firm to achieve the goal of changing the rent. At the same time, a custody committee was organized to deposit the rent to be paid into a bank for safekeeping. The representatives were scheduled to meet with the landlord in person to ask him to consider the current economic downturn in the French Concession, which has reached its extreme, and to consider reducing the rent burden to provide relief and maintain commerce.

Street Ruffians Corrupt Morality and Humiliate Women 160

Two Incidents of Respectable Women Feeling Deeply Embarrassed Occurred in One Day

丨Arrests Made and Stern Punishment Handed Down by the Court丨

Idlers and vagrants are most numerous in the concessions of this city. These people do nothing all day long except call friends and roam the streets. When they see young women, whether they are noble ladies, famous courtesans, or dissolute women, they all flirt with them, corrupting morality and insulting women. Almost every day this happens. The day before yesterday, two incidents occurred in succession: (1) Qin Jinyuan, accompanied by his wife, Gao, and his relative Chen Tan, was walking near the intersection of Danshui Road and Fuxu Road when Zhang Chengyan, a man from Pudong, suddenly saw that the two women were quite attractive and stopped them to make jokes and say obscene words. He also reached out and touched Gao's left leg. Qin scolded him severely. Zhang became angry out of shame and, in an instant, gathered seven or eight of his gang members and surrounded the Qin couple. Without any discussion, they began to beat them. Although Qin and his wife resisted, they were no match and were all injured. The gang then dispersed. When the police arrived after hearing the alarm, most of them had fled far away. Only Zhang Chengyan, the leader, was arrested and taken to the Xinzha Police Station for detention. (2) Wang Yingxiang and his wife, Wang Fengying, and his wife's younger sister, Wang Er'e, were walking to the intersection of Weihaiwei Road and Muming Road. Wang Yingxiang had a sudden urge to urinate and went into a nearby alley, asking his wife to wait by the roadside. It was already dusk. Wang Er'e, a man from Hangzhou, happened to pass by and saw this pair of beautiful women standing gracefully under the electric lights. He suddenly had a wicked thought and thought it was a great opportunity to lure them. He stepped forward and pretended to be attentive, trying to force them to go to a hotel with him. Just as the Wang sisters were in a predicament, Wang Yingxiang came out of the alley. Upon learning that his wife's younger sister had been harassed, he argued with Wang Er'e. Wang then let out a shout, and his gang members suddenly arrived. They then started fighting, and the Wang couple suffered minor injuries. They then reported it to the Jing'an Temple Road Police Station, and detective Qian Xianting arrested Wang Er'e. Yesterday morning, he was brought to the First Special District Local Court together with Zhang Chengyan. Judge Wang Ren conducted a preliminary hearing. The police lawyer Chen Baolian stated the facts of the case, saying that both defendants were being charged with assault and requested strict punishment. Qin and Wang, along with their families and witnesses, came to court to testify about the situation at the time. When questioned, the defendants all pleaded guilty and did not make any excuses. After the interrogation, Judge Wang immediately announced the verdict, sentencing Zhang Chengyan to four months of imprisonment and Wang Er'e to two months of imprisonment, as a warning.

Impersonating a Military Commission Staff Member and Riding the Train Without a Ticket 161

The Official Documents and Symbols Were All Forged, Confessed to Being Purchased for 30 Yuan, Involving Elementary School Teacher Chen Mou, Who Has Been Arrested and Will Be Transferred

On the 26th of last month, He Jinqian, dressed in military uniform and wearing symbols, boarded a train from Shanghai to Beijing without buying a ticket. He was interrogated by the military police stationed on the train. He claimed to be a staff member of the Military Commission's rear hospital and was going to Beijing on official business. He immediately took out a document from the rear hospital. Upon closer inspection, the military police found that the text and symbols were all forged, and he was undoubtedly impersonating a military officer. He was placed under guard. When the train arrived in Nanjing, he was escorted to the Capital Garrison Command. After a preliminary interrogation by a military judge, He confessed that he had paid 30 yuan to Chen Yuanding, a teacher at Renci Elementary School at No. 181, De'an Lane, North Shanxi Road, a Shaoxing native, to introduce him to Shen Lijun. Shen gave him the uniform and symbols, claiming that he was the director of the Military Commission's rear hospital and was sending him to Beijing on important business.

New Invention to Prevent Car Theft 162

According to the Shanghai Times, 27,000 of the 28,000 bicycles in this city may have been received some good news. It is reported that an inventor in this city has invented a new design that can prevent car thieves from using their methods. The main mechanism is in a small iron box, installed behind the triangle frame, and connected to the rear wheel. If the car owner parks the car on the road, he only needs to turn the key, and if someone moves the car or causes the rear wheel to turn, the box will immediately emit a warning similar to a ship's whistle. The thief will definitely abandon the car and run away in fright when he suddenly hears the loud noise. When the car owner moves the car, he only needs to turn the key in the opposite direction to drive away safely without making a warning sound.

The Headquarters obtained this information and sent a letter to the Shanghai Public Security Bureau, requesting assistance in the arrest. At 10:30 am the day before yesterday, Supervisor Fu Sucun of the Municipal Public Security Bureau first reported to the Huishi Police Station. Together with Chinese Detective Shen Dehui, they arrested Chen Yuanding at Renci Elementary School in De'an Lane, while Shen Lijun had already fled after hearing the news. Chen was taken back to the police station for detention. Yesterday morning, he was sent to the Criminal Division of the First Special District Court. The police lawyer Li Zhishan stated the above situation, saying that the defendant, Chen Yuanding, was arrested by the Municipal Public Security Bureau based on the confession of the criminal He Jinqian, who was apprehended by the Nanjing Garrison Command. Now, the Municipal Public Security Bureau has sent representatives to the case, requesting transfer. The police station also has no objections. Then, Supervisor Fu Sucun of the Municipal Public Security Bureau reported the circumstances of the joint arrest and requested the transfer, saying that the official documents of the Public Security Bureau were not prepared in advance and were not brought to the case. They would be submitted in the afternoon. Chen Yuanding claimed that he did not know He Jinqian, but that Shen Lijun was introduced to him by a friend. Therefore, he was completely unaware of He's actions. He also hired a lawyer to defend him in court. After verifying the confession, Judge Liu Yugui ordered Chen Yuanding to be temporarily detained in the detention center of this court, pending the arrival of the transfer documents from the Municipal Public Security Bureau, which would be transferred immediately to the case for interrogation.

Two People Committed Suicide by Drowning in the Huangpu River 163

丨One Man and One Woman, Both Due to Economic Pressure丨

The day before yesterday evening, one man and one woman jumped into the Huangpu River one after another to commit suicide. The man was due to economic pressure, and the woman was due to poverty and illness. Fortunately, both were rescued. They are recorded below:

Li Xiushan 164

Li Xiushan, a 20-year-old native of Zhaopu, lives at No. 11 Haining Road. He has a father, a stepmother, and two older brothers. Because Li only engaged in lowly activities and did not strive for progress, his father ordered him to learn the printing business in order to prepare to open a shop in the future. However, good advice grates on the ear, and Li dropped out halfway, which led to him being looked down upon by his family. Li wanted to live a life of leisure but could not, and the money in his hand became increasingly tight, so he had a pessimistic thought. At 5:45 PM on the day before yesterday, he boarded ferry No. 10 at the New Customs Wharf and crossed to the Huangpu River. Li immediately jumped into the raging waves to commit suicide. Fortunately, he was rescued by the ferry captain and sent to the Customs Water Police Station. After the police chief learned the truth, he ordered patrolman Huang Songsheng to send him home.

Chen Hu 165

At 7:45 PM the night before last, a middle-aged woman jumped into the river from the Zhejiang Road Bridge on Suzhou Creek to commit suicide. Fortunately, she was spotted by a Chinese policeman at the Customs Water Police Station, who immediately took steps to rescue her and took her to the police station. She claimed that her name was Chen Hu, 33 years old, from Hangzhou, and lived in the Pinle Tea Garden in the French Concession. She had no family in Shanghai, was lonely, and very poor. She had also been ill for many days and had no money to see a doctor. Unable to bear the suffering, she sought death. The police chief, feeling very sorry for her, ordered patrolman Qu Hekui to send her to Renji Hospital for treatment first and then find ways to help her.

Stray Bullet from Italian Navy Target Practice Kills Lü Yuanquan 173

Lü Yuanquan, a 42-year-old resident of Jiading, lived at No. 1355 Yuyuan Road. He came from a well-off family. Lü also owned a flower garden at No. 2 Xitiyuhui Road, Jiangwan Road, Zhabei, where he hired craftsmen to plant flowers and trees. He also built several elegant houses there, which he used as a place to relax and cultivate his nature, living a very contented life. At around 10 o'clock yesterday morning, Lü again took a car from his home to the flower garden. When passing near the target range of Hongkou Park at the end of North Sichuan Road, the Italian Marine Corps was practicing live-fire target practice at that location. Lü, thinking that he was far enough away, did not detour. Suddenly, a stray bullet hit him in the head. The bullet entered from Lü's forehead and exited from the back of his head. Brain matter flowed out with the bullet, and he died instantly. Villagers discovered the incident and immediately reported it to the Fifth District Public Security Bureau, which dispatched police to the scene. A business card was found near the deceased, revealing his surname and address. Officials were dispatched to report to his family, and the local court was notified to send someone to examine the body.

Record of Trial of Tiangong Blood Case 178

The blood case that occurred at the Tiangong Barber Shop at No. 177 Chongqing Road

was investigated by the police, who arrested four suspects: Zhao Heming (19 years old), Chen Muzhou (19 years old), Wu Luzhi (17 years old), and Qiu Gengsheng (21 years old). They were escorted to the First Court of the Special District the day before yesterday. The circumstances of the trial by Judge Wu Tingqi have already been recorded in this newspaper. Because the bodies were to be examined that day, the trial was adjourned to yesterday afternoon for continued hearing. Police lawyer Li Zhishan stated the circumstances of the case, in addition to what had already been stated, he also said that the third and fourth defendants had confessed to beating and assaulting the victim at the police station. Chen Muzhou also joined in the beating, and Zhao Heming confessed that he had heard about the fight beforehand. Then, the owner of the Tiangong Barber Shop, Ruan Ming, testified that he knew that his partners Chen Bingnan and Luo Wanqing had caused a conflict by hitting someone with a bicycle. He was about to order Chen and Luo to ask someone to mediate when the incident occurred in the shop. Because he was not on the scene when the incident occurred, he did not know who had done it. Then, the detective in charge of the case presented the white inner and outer clothing worn by the deceased in court. It was clear that there was a tear on the right chest and shoulder, stained with blood. When questioned, the four defendants either claimed that they were playing in the area, or that they only knew about the fight and did not commit the assault. Judge Wu wanted to investigate the case further and ordered the police to investigate eyewitnesses among the neighbors to clarify the truth. The trial was adjourned to the 29th of this month for further hearing.

nature and enthusiastically supported local public welfare undertakings. Wen Hongen Talks About the Dispute at Quanzhang Middle School 180

A reporter from the Xinxin News Agency inquired about the truth of the case where Yang Jingshi, Ye Qinghe, and others falsely reported to the Public Security Bureau that the Quanzhang Guild Hall had sent police to arrest and injure students of Quanzhang Middle School, and posted an emergency notice in the newspaper seeking assistance from all sectors. Yesterday, they specially visited Director Wen of the Public Security Bureau to inquire about the truth of the case. The conversation is recorded as follows: (Question) Did Yang Liangshi expel the principal and falsely report that the students were reactionary, and did the Public Security Bureau send police to search the school? (Answer) The faculty and staff of Quanzhang Middle School were previously divided into different factions, and some students were used to attack each other, resulting in disturbances. Later, upon order, the school was temporarily closed by the Education Bureau because the school's members were complex and there were indeed reactionaries inciting them. As for sending police to search, that was not true. (Question) Did the Public Security Bureau send armed police to arrest students and falsely accuse them of being communists at the request of Yang Jingshi? (Answer) After Quanzhang Middle School was closed, a small number of students still occupied the school, and more than 30 students who were not originally from the school were recruited to the school, intending to cause trouble. The Education Bureau approved the Municipal Government to dissolve the school's students together with police officers of this bureau. Later, the number of students gathered more and more, nearly a hundred people. Not only did they not listen to the dissolution order, but they also summoned people from outside the school to openly hold a meeting, establishing the prohibited National Resistance to Insults Self-Salvation Association, Quanzhang Branch, South Shanghai District. On April 13, more than ten students beat and injured the guard hired by the school and the school servant stationed at the school. Because the students occupying the school had acted excessively, the Education Bureau sent a letter requesting that the students staying at the school be released on bail separately. If they were not good members, they would be dismissed from the school by the board of directors with the assistance of their fellow villagers. However, the students still ignored the order, and various transgressions occurred from time to time. This bureau believed that the situation was urgent, so on the 19th of this month, it ordered police officers to go to enforce the dissolution in order to maintain public security. After the officers repeatedly persuaded them, the students remained deaf to them and dared to resist and shout, and threw chairs and benches. The momentum was fierce, and it seemed that they wanted to seize weapons. On the same day, police officer Wang Tongjie of the Rihuigang Branch, etc., were all beaten at the same time. Police chief Xu Rongbin's right arm and police officer Liu Huaifa's left leg were injured by sticks and benches. As a last resort, the police officers brought the rioting students Wu Zhen, etc., 45 people, and the school servant Chen Azhong, etc., who participated in the riot, to the bureau. Five kinds of communist propaganda materials were found in the school courtyard. When the students were brought to the bureau, they dared to shout "Long live the Communist Party". After separate interrogations, they all admitted to defying the dissolution order and obstructing official duties. The criminals, evidence, leaflets, and confessions have all been transferred to the court for handling. As for the request made by Yang Jingshi, that did not happen. (Xinxin News Agency)

Central Bank Inspection Report No. 161 181

The Central Bank's 161st Inspection Report on Issuance Reserves states:

According to Article 15 of the Central Bank Regulations, the Council is responsible for inspecting the reserve funds for the issuance of convertible notes by the Bank. The 161st inspection was held at the Issuance Bureau of the Bank on May 20, 1933. The results of the inspection are announced as follows: (A) Total amount of convertible notes issued: 45,173,346 silver dollars, including: 40,887,749 silver dollar notes, 4,285,597 subsidiary coin notes, Total amount of convertible note reserves: 45,173,346 silver dollars, including: 37,071,446 silver dollars in cash reserves. The cash reserves are: 32,242,377 silver dollars stored in the Bank's issuing vault, 3,092,596 silver dollars stored in branches in various ports, 1,779,373 silver dollars stored in the same industry, Guarantee reserves are equivalent to 8,059,000 silver dollars. (B,)

Total amount of customs gold convertible notes issued: 417,269.4 yuan, Total amount of customs gold convertible note reserves: 417,269.4 yuan. The reserve fund includes 7,004 taels and 6.9 cents of bullion, equivalent to 417,269.4 yuan of customs gold at a price of 5957. According to Article 2 of the Central Bank's Convertible Note Regulations, 60% of the cash reserve and 40% of the guarantee reserve. The results of this inspection show that the cash exceeds 60% and the guarantee is less than 40%, which is in line with the regulations. This report is hereby made. May 20, 1933, Chairman of the Board of Supervisors of the Central Bank, Li Fusun, Supervisors Wang Jingli, Bei Songsun, Qin Runqing, Lin Kanghou, Xu Jiluan.

Reader Advisor 193

Marriage Troubles 194

| Letter from Mr. Wu Yitian of Wuxian County |

I am from the northern part of Wuxian County. My father died early, and my mother is still alive. My family is extremely poor. Our daily life depends solely on my mother's domestic work income. I studied old-style books for three years when I was young. At the age of twelve, my mother sent me to a small town to learn the business of ramie and sundries stores. In less than a year, I ran away home because I couldn't bear the abuse of the store owner and his wife. That year, my mother arranged for me to be engaged to a Xue girl from a neighboring family, who was illiterate and very foolish, in a compulsory manner. At that time, due to my level of knowledge and the constraints of traditional shame, I silently acquiesced without any resistance. Later, a diligent fellow villager often lent me various books and, a year later, registered me for a rural normal school and encouraged me to take the entrance exam. Fortunately, I passed the exam this time, and thus began my school life. In the winter of that year, my mother again forced me to marry the Xue girl, and I repeatedly refused. Unexpectedly, my mother cut off my financial support, and I was immediately in danger of dropping out of school. Considering this, I had no choice but to obey my mother's orders and go through a marriage ceremony. However, in those ten years, I never had any physical relationship with her, I can swear to heaven. After graduation, I became a teacher, then a principal, and then obtained a small leadership position as a low-level autonomous worker. Last winter, we both understood the pain of not being able to cooperate at all. Why ruin the future happiness of both of us? We both realized this and proposed divorce terms, obtained the consent of both parties, had a lawyer certify it, and filed it with the court. After going through legal procedures, both parties voluntarily dissolved the marital relationship, which was not a difficult problem. However, the general remnants of feudalism relentlessly attacked me, believing that a wife who has shared hardship should not be divorced, and that this act was a heinous crime and a degradation of personality. Editor, please say a fair word! What do you think of my behavior! Can marriage problems be compromised? Or should they be taken seriously? This is unexpected, "one wave has not subsided, and another wave rises again!" Since my divorce, due to the intense nature of my autonomous work, I have had few opportunities to get close to young women of equal thoughts and knowledge. Therefore, a classmate, Du, introduced me to a Yang girl from an old-fashioned family, who was said to be able to read and write a little, of excellent character, and able to manage the household in an orderly manner. I believed it to be true, thinking that Du was my old classmate and would never deceive me. He also took me to the Jiang girl's house for a meal. At that time, limited by the walls of feudal society! Before the conventions of men and women meeting freely had been broken, I still felt it was inconvenient to talk to the Jiang girl. This time, I only gained the impression that "the inside is unknown, but the appearance is acceptable." Therefore, on that day, I exchanged photos and miscellaneous items through a matchmaker and paid a deposit of ten yuan, preparing to send the betrothal gifts on a fixed date, almost completing the initial work of an old-fashioned marriage. In less than a few days, I learned of many unpleasant things, such as being unchaste! Illiterate! Bad family history! I immediately expressed my refusal and stopped the process. Afterwards, the Jiang girl's father, instead, crazily negotiated directly with me, demanding compensation for reputational and material losses. Recently, I have been feeling overwhelmed and mentally confused. If it comes to litigation, I cannot produce the kind of evidence that "there is a cause, but no evidence is found" in court, and I have no legal certainty, and my position may be shaken as a result. If I want to settle the matter peacefully, the other party's harsh conditions are difficult to accept. This matter has reached a stalemate, and it is difficult to resolve it well. I implore the knowledgeable and experienced editor to quickly think of a proper solution for me and indicate the path I should take. And how can I find a lover in the future? Is there any hope for satisfaction in this transitional period?

Answer: Your letter has been read and understood, and I will reply briefly as follows: (1) Marriage problems cannot be compromised; (2) You formed an acquaintance with her and even got engaged simply based on what others said about her being good; when others said she was bad, you had problems with her: what "many unpleasant things," what "unchaste," what "illiterate," what "bad family history," causing you to lose your mind, which shows that you are a person who "relies on ears instead of eyes" and has no opinion of your own. Now that the person is in front of you, you can interact with her, "seeing is believing, hearing is deceiving." Is she really "illiterate"? Are there really many unpleasant things? Even if she lost her virginity in the past, but she sincerely loves you now, what does it matter? How bad is the family history? Was she a prostitute? Was she secretly promiscuous? Even if so, what direct relationship does it have with her? Even if she herself was bad in the past, but she now shows herself to be a self-loving and upward-striving person in her actions, should her present good qualities be buried because of her past deeds? Frankly speaking, "a prodigal son who returns is worth more than gold." If I didn't have a wife, I would definitely look for a woman who was "bad" in the past but has now repented, a woman who was "unchaste" in the past but now wholeheartedly wants to be a good person, and reject those unmarried ladies who think they are flawless and pure as jade. Because the latter have never experienced the world, have never been in the dirty society, that is to say, have never been to the testing ground, no one can guarantee whether they will stumble in the future. On the other hand, the former have already tasted the bitterness of bad society, and as the saying goes, "know all the true and false feelings of people." Now that they have come to their senses and "laid down the butcher knife," they are looking for a place to settle down. If you get along with them, they will definitely be considerate and give you a lot of comfort. In the past, there was a scholar whose wife died. He wrote a letter to a friend saying that he was preparing to look for a widow to remarry. Someone asked him why, and he said that a widow had experienced the death of her husband and must know the pain of losing a husband. Now that she is marrying again, she will definitely know how to cherish her husband. Although his words are close to jest, there is indeed a profound truth in them, which I will use to tell you. In short: make up your own mind and never "eat mutton when you fall east, and eat dog meat when you fall west."

Page 13

Spring and Autumn

Eccentric Rejects Birthday Celebrations 195

— Zhan Lu

The world's three great eccentrics are, in Italy, Mussolini; in Germany, Hitler; and in Japan, Araki Sadao.

If one were to write a comparative essay on these three, Araki Sadao's eccentric score would probably not pass. He only knows how to bully weak countries, where is the eccentricity in that? The eccentric status of Italy's Mussolini has been maintained for a long time, and it is still flourishing. Recently, he has been showing his face on the political stage, with an arrogant air of invincibility, scaring away Einstein, the inventor of "relativity," and frightening many "Shylock"-style Jewish tycoons who exploit heavy profits. Even his words have attracted the attention of the world's powers. If his tone is peaceful, the powers seem to be reassured; if his tone is fierce, the powers frown as if a catastrophe is about to erupt. Alas! The prime minister of a defeated country is so valued, Hitler's eccentricity is simply a well-deserved eccentricity!

Last month, on a certain day, was the forty-fourth birthday of the eccentric Hitler. A powerful minister celebrating his birthday is, of course, a good way to make a fortune. But look, which powerful ministers in Chinese history did not celebrate their birthdays lavishly? A group of servile and obsequious subordinates and officials could take this opportunity to bring gold to the powerful's door and lobby for good positions in front of the birthday celebrant. As long as one birthday is celebrated, the "birthday tribute" from all directions will bring in countless gold, jewels, and treasures. Even second- and third-rate dignitaries who are not powerful or not ministers are unwilling to miss this opportunity to make a fortune on their birthdays. No matter how much the public laughs and scolds, the birthday celebrant will do it his own way, this is a traditional mindset of Chinese officials.

Too much has been said, straying from the topic of this article. After all, does Hitler celebrate his birthday or not? On his birthday, German President Hindenburg presented him with a personally signed silver-framed photograph, such an extraordinary honor that it seemed necessary to celebrate his birthday lavishly. However, he actually rejected the birthday celebrations. However, although he rejected the birthday celebrations, the public insisted on celebrating his birthday for him. On this day, all the newspapers in the country had a special section on Hitler. The National Socialist Party headquarters received a continuous stream of congratulatory telegrams from all directions. Party members and the Steel Helmet League participated in a review in front of the Berlin Ministry of Interior. All government agencies hung flags to celebrate, and in the evening there was a grand lantern parade. The people supported him to such an extent, which is something the eccentric can be proud of.

A fine old Chinese man who relies on celebrating birthdays to make a fortune sneered: Hitler, although you have the support of the people, but by refusing to celebrate your own birthday, you have missed an opportunity to make a fortune. You are not a birthday celebrant, you are a fool.

The Sorrow of the Fat Miss 196

— Zui Chi Sheng

Miss X next door graduated from middle school and is lonely at home. One day, she saw an advertisement in the newspaper saying, "XX Company is recruiting female staff," which touched her heartstrings. She excitedly ran to the company to register for the exam. On the day of the exam, Miss X changed into a brand new fashionable cheongsam, brought some necessary items, and became a member of the examinees. At that time, there were middle-aged women, modern girls, beautiful and ugly, crowding a room. Of course, they were all hoping to "seek women's economic independence." Everyone managed to write a vernacular essay and a letter, and then left the venue. The person in charge told them: Come back in three days to hear the results. Three days later, in the afternoon, Miss X excitedly ran back to hear the news. The person in charge of the company said to her: Our company has already selected several female staff members, with a monthly salary of fourteen yuan, all of whom are "graceful and slender" modern ladies. Your level, madam, is indeed not bad. However, your figure is too fat, so you failed. This is related to the business of our company, so we have to be strict in our selection. Miss X was ashamed and angry when she heard this, turned around and left. She could still vaguely hear someone saying: A big lump like that also wants to be a "flower vase," she really doesn't know her place.

Miss X was extremely angry, looked around, as if the world

was too narrow, and her body seemed to be magnified several times, and quietly went home. She didn't eat dinner and cried all night.

Meritorious Dog 197

— Bing Ding

Dogs have no country, they are not required to fulfill the obligations of "serving in the military" and paying taxes, and they certainly do not enjoy the rights of "slaves of a fallen country." Of course, humans cannot compare to dogs. Moreover, there are now dogs that can make movies: dog stars | dogs that protect wealthy people: police dogs | dogs that help hunters: hunting dogs | and dogs that contribute to the country: meritorious dogs |. The great achievements of dogs are, after all, impressive, and of course, humans cannot compare to dogs. For those who have contributed to the country, of course, they should be rewarded according to their merits. Even ancestral sacrifices and temple worship for thousands of years are the duties that cannot be shirked. Because Zeng Disheng's Xiang Army broke Nanjing, many people died, so he built the Xiang Army Zhaozhong Temple in Nanjing. He also wrote a great article to praise the loyalty of the Xiang Army who died in battle. During the January 28th Incident, many members of the 19th Route Army who resisted the Japanese army died, and some people initiated the establishment of a Tomb of Unknown Heroes. Only when it comes to rewarding animals for their merits, we Chinese people have never thought of it. It is already unfortunate to be a Chinese, but it is even more unfortunate to be a Chinese dog or horse.

It is said: "The Japanese military has decided to implement meritorious rewards for military animals from June 1st. The categories are divided into A, B, and C. The animals to be rewarded are military horses, military dogs, and military pigeons. For these animals that died for the country, a memorial hall will be established in Zojo-ji Temple in Shiba Park, and they will be enshrined in this hall." I think that the Japanese treat dogs and horses that died for the country so generously, and their Japanese dogs and horses will certainly serve the country as well as the Japanese. Returning to the topic, our noble country has not built temples or set up spirits for these animals that died for the country. Their loyal souls wander, and they have to use the heavens and earth as their coffins and the sun and moon as their burial shrouds. If the souls of beasts have knowledge, they will also sigh that they are inferior to Japanese dogs and horses.

North Station 198

— Ke Ding'an

Far away, the sound of the呜呜 whistle of the train is heard, and the train like a long snake, meandering and slowly enters the platform: a burst of noisy sounds suddenly rise, at this time, there are single travelers, very lightly carrying a briefcase, quickly jumping down, walking out of the platform, that is to say, they have arrived in Shanghai, without any troublesome events, there are also single people, but they bring a lot of cumbersome luggage, some on their shoulders, some on their arms, some in their hands, but they really feel the bitterness of going out, some bring their wives or children, and also bring a lot of luggage and odds and ends, and also want to save money, so troublesome events occur, their own things, it is not good to ask their wives to take them, it is not strong enough to ask their children to take them, in this situation, I know that they feel very distressed, there are also comfortable friends, on the train, just a greeting to the workers wearing round-topped hats, and they will peacefully take your things, walk out of the platform, but you have to pay attention, the tip for them, can not be too little, nor too much: too little, they will think you are "stingy," too much, they will think you are "a sucker." In front of the luggage cart, it also becomes a noisy market, the workers, in the carriages, stack and throw the luggage of others, which is not their own, one by one on the platform, if you bring three pieces of luggage, then to find it as your own, it will take at least a quarter of an hour, of course, it is an exception if it is placed in a place where you can see it, they will scatter your three pieces of luggage, and also push your luggage with the luggage of others, making it difficult for you to check, this is about the platform,

When you walk out of the platform, although there is now a

rope apart, but the mouths of the hotel staff are not sealed. They are still shouting and yelling, disturbing people's eardrums. There are also general self-offering diligent carriage, car, rickshaw touts to solicit you, carry luggage for you, take parts, so that you have to take his car, if you agree to his request, then you will at least have to compare

The price is more than double the usual hire, and sometimes it will make your luggage disappear.

Now, the Public Security Bureau has finally made a regulation that rickshaws are not allowed to stop in front of the station, otherwise, the rickshaw encirclement will also be unbearable. This is about the outside of the North Station.

The characteristics of the North Station are originally like this!

Four Company Commanders of the Northeast 199

— Zhang Henshui

Chapter Seven: Several words sever affection and close the door to weep in pain; one shoulder bears righteousness and discuss matters over wine.

Jiang said: On the first day of the new year, I should also invite him to eat something. Please trouble Zhao Company Commander to tell him, I am waiting here. Zhao Company Commander

Zhao Weng smiled and arranged everyone properly, and said with a smile: I am very happy to see you brothers so strong and vigorous, but every time you are here laughing and joking, I am very happy, but after you all leave, I am very lonely, so it is better if you don't come. Yin Deren scratched his hair and smiled slightly: Old people like excitement, but I don't think so. If you don't want any excitement at all, you naturally don't know what it means to be indifferent. Zhao Weng smiled and said: Because of this, you don't take a company commander's wife. But when you are carrying a gun, you can not want a wife, but when you retire to your hometown in the future, you still don't want a wife? Look at me, so old, only alone, living in this half-rural, half-town place: he said to this place, fearing that his son would have any misunderstanding, took a look, he smiled slightly: This is what I say again, I am just afraid of being alone, so I moved here to be close to Ziqiang. You are not married now, where did the son come from, when you reach my age in the future, see if you are lonely? Tian Qing took out a small white handkerchief from the small pocket of his suit, placed it on his knee, folded it endlessly, but a slight smile appeared on his face. Zhao Weng thought he had some discussion, touched the long beard under his chin, and looked at him and said: Company Commander Tian, ​​you are the youngest, you must hear what I said, right? Zhao Ziqiang was afraid that his father would talk and talk, and would talk about his own marriage problem, so he repeatedly said: The dishes are all ready, let's eat. As he spoke, he was busy setting up bowls, chopsticks, and chairs on the table in the middle room, making a gesture of not having time to pay attention to what others were saying. (79)

The Voice of National Salvation

National Scholars Should Quickly Establish Standards for Saving the Country 200

— Continued by Zhuan

I have heard that all things have a fixed standard, and the issue of saving the country is certainly no exception. A standard means that within a certain scope, there must be a certain number of things that can be done, and within that scope, there must also be a certain number of things that cannot be done. If clear standards can be established for saving the country, then people of average ability will know what to do, and outstanding individuals will also know where to stop. Overly ambitious pursuits are unacceptable, and so is being weak and shrinking back. National crisis is something that no one has experienced. When troops are lost and territory is seized, students across the country often display a sense of helplessness. Students at one school want to volunteer for the army, while students at another school want to buy airplanes for war preparedness. Some truly rush to the front lines, while others truly donate all their savings. This is what Mencius meant by "human nature is inherently good; if it can be fully developed, it is enough to protect the entire world." The ignorant fail to observe this, saying that the effort is too small for the task and that it is like a drop in the bucket. Yet, no one loudly calls for the continuous establishment of standards for saving the country in academic circles. This is a major issue that both new and old scholars should pay close attention to. It should start with one school taking the lead, and then other schools will follow suit. For example, if a fire breaks out in someone's house, the fire has already started, and everyone in the family is in a panic. Some even leave valuable clothing chests untouched and only grab a rice pot from the kitchen. We cannot blame them for lacking the ability to move furniture; we should excuse their lack of experience with house fires. However, the Shanghai Fire Brigade is different. When a fire breaks out outside, the firefighters are fully prepared and armed, waiting. When the lookout tower rings an alarm bell, the fire engine has already arrived outside the door. Upon hearing the bell indicating the direction and street, they immediately rush to the fire scene to fight the fire. In an orderly manner, each person performs their duty, and the fire will certainly not spread. The helplessness of students at various schools is like grabbing a rice pot during a fire. And the establishment of standards for saving the country by new and old scholars across the country is like establishing a fire brigade.

The enmity between Germany and France has led to several times in 130 years where they have bet their entire country.

However, the German philosophy professor Hegel, at the University of Jena, on the day in 1806 when Napoleon led his troops to invade, held his manuscript in the lecture hall and looked out the window, jokingly commenting on Napoleon as the "world spirit" (I saw a cartoon of this in the new edition of the Encyclopedia Britannica).

This was the attitude of a philosophy professor during a national crisis in Germany. Also, the German chemistry professor Louis Pasteur, who took refuge in Arbois, said on the day in 1870 when Bismarck designated the annexation of Alsace and Lorraine: "Desperate efforts in a laboratory are just like being on a battlefield." This was the attitude of a science professor during a national crisis in France. Both of these men became prominent figures who enriched their countries with philosophy and science. It is truly said that "adversity awakens the wise, and hardship strengthens a nation." New scholars in our country are familiar with this kind of history and will surely find many pieces of evidence in books, which can also serve as materials for establishing standards for saving the country.

As for the old scholars, I want to loudly awaken them and say: Do not

appoint yourselves to wait for the right time like Wang Tong and Chen Bu, and do not appoint yourselves to restore the country after a hundred years like Gu Tinglin and Huang Lizhou. Today's national crisis is not a small domestic political turmoil; it is a national crisis of becoming slaves and being exterminated as a race. You must appoint yourselves like Guan Zhong and Yue Yi, like the followers of Mozi, You Qin Huali, and like Liu Bei, a follower of Zheng Xuan, and like Shi Kefa, a follower of Zuo Guangdou. And you must never lecture on the "Great Learning" in a boat at Yai Shan, allowing Yan Xizhai to criticize you for reading dead books. If "LIBERTY" is translated as "仁" (benevolence), how could the entire country's moral principles be so unrestrained? If "EQUALITY" is translated as "義" (righteousness), how could the entire country's order be so chaotic? Individualists emphasize that their efforts should come from themselves, not that they must exclusively enjoy the benefits. The sanctity of labor emphasizes that goods should not be abandoned, not that butchers are living Buddhas. Materialists use raw materials to develop things and refine manufacturing to accomplish tasks, not to just "buy things." The process of natural selection involves internal cooperation and external competition, not "abandoning etiquette and concession." Those who grasp these key points should have the wisdom of Zhuge Liang, the foresight of Fan Zhongyan, the talent of Wang Yangming, the scholarship of Weng Wenduan, and the good governance of Lin Zexu. With the power of a short message, they can influence the vision and hearing of China. Why wait to lecture before understanding? Alas! When people are in dire straits, they call out to heaven; when they are in pain, they call out to their parents. During the Xinhai Revolution, there was a call for "humanitarianism" from both Chinese and Westerners. However, the Beiyang warlord Yuan Shikai and his ilk followed Sun Yat-sen's model. This time, the League of Nations investigation includes a call for "national character." If it succeeds, will heaven repent and change disaster? Will the country have hope? This is what all Chinese people should possess: a spirit of "turning the tide and transforming the world."

Important Education News 201

Wang Shijie Discusses the Safety of Schools in Tianjin and Peiping

Studying Appropriate Response Methods; Schools Strictly Ordered to Maintain Calm

(Nanjing, 23rd) Minister of Education Wang Shijie discussed the critical situation in North China. The

Ministry is extremely concerned about the safety of universities in Tianjin and Peiping, fearing that students at various schools

will panic and disturb each other. He has strictly ordered all schools to maintain calm, continue classes as usual, or hold exams, and not to leave school or suspend classes lightly. As for the issue of schools moving south, appropriate response methods are currently being studied and will be submitted to the Executive Yuan for approval. However, a decision is unlikely to be made before the summer vacation.

Jiangsu Provincial Government Resolves to Instruct the Department of Education to Actively Prepare for the Joint Examination 203

Individuals Unwilling to Take the Exam May Do So, But Will Not Be Issued Graduation Diplomas

The Jiangsu Provincial Government resolved yesterday that it was deeply alarmed by reports that a small number of students in the province were opposed to the graduation joint examination. It instructed the Department of Education to continue actively preparing for it, carefully formulate methods, and properly conduct it. Individuals who are unwilling to take the exam may do so at their own discretion, but according to the Ministry's order, they will not be issued graduation diplomas. Schools may also not issue certificates similar to diplomas. Those who incite unrest, obstruct others from taking the exam, and disrupt the joint examination system will be considered to be defying national government orders and disrupting social order and should be severely punished to curb the source of chaos.

With the sound of horns and drums, the warhorses leap forward, *Shen Bao*'s frontline is greatly invigorated. Little Zhang of *Shi Bao* is so enraged that flames shoot from his nostrils and smoke billows from all seven orifices.

Sun Daosheng Captures Fang La Single-Handedly
