Special Feature

Recent Reforms in Elementary and Secondary School Curriculum and Educational Administration in Soviet Russia (1) by Zhu Zhensun 224

I. The Failure of School Education in Soviet Russia

Since the promulgation of compulsory education laws and the implementation of revised curricula, Soviet Russia has indeed achieved considerable success in elementary and secondary school education. This is acknowledged by the Central Committee of the Communist Party of Soviet Russia. However, Soviet Russian schools still suffer from many shortcomings. The most important of these is the inability of schools to provide basic knowledge in subjects such as biology, physics, chemistry, mathematics, national languages, geography, and other subjects necessary for preparation for admission to higher and specialized schools. The main reasons for this failure are the inadequacy of the curriculum (especially the curriculum for higher grades), poor classroom teaching methods, lack of guidance from the education commission and its agencies, and the lack of rigorous training in schools. In addition, there is another shortcoming, namely, the inability to unify the school system. As a result, elementary and secondary schools often fail to meet the needs of compulsory subjects for admission to higher education.

II. Recent Revisions of the Curriculum

In view of the shortcomings in schools, the Central Committee of the Communist Party of Soviet Russia passed a resolution on September 5, 1931, to improve the secondary school curriculum. Since then, the curriculum of elementary and secondary schools, especially the curriculum of elementary schools, has been considerably improved, and the content of the curriculum has become more substantial than before. However, the Central Committee found that there were still certain shortcomings in the curriculum, so it finally proposed to revise the curriculum for the fifth, sixth, and seventh grades. They believe that the curriculum for these three grades has the following shortcomings:

(1) The amount of content is too much, and as a result, students can only quickly acquire a small amount of superficial knowledge from the subjects. For example, this is especially true of the part of solid geometry in the seventh grade mathematics subject.

(2) The teaching materials are not consistent with each other. For example, the teaching materials for mathematics and drawing, as well as the teaching materials for mathematics, physics, chemistry, and manual labor, are all inconsistent. Therefore, the geometry knowledge required for drawing assignments in the fifth grade is not taught until the sixth grade. Furthermore, in higher grades, physics often lacks the necessary foundation of mathematical knowledge.

(3) Some subjects are oversimplified. For example, citing Newton's laws in physics and explaining the structure of cells in biology are often the cases. Furthermore, in geography, students generally do not have sufficient opportunities to observe maps. In social science, many political errors often occur.

(4) Social science often does not pay attention to historical facts, so there is little description of the land and social evolution of mankind in the past. There is also a major shortcoming in that they have not yet prepared a historical curriculum.

As a result, the Central Committee of the Communist Party recommended to the Education Committee of the Soviet Russian Republic that it revise all the curricula of elementary and secondary schools starting from January 1, 1933, so as to provide students with a systematic knowledge of the three "R"s (reading, writing, and arithmetic). These curriculum revisions are based on the following principles:

(A) The teaching materials for mathematics, physics, chemistry, and biology, whether in terms of scope or nature, should be suitable for the age of the relevant class. The teaching materials for many subjects should be reduced so that a solid foundation can be laid in these basic training areas.

(B) The teaching materials for mathematics, physics, and chemistry, as well as the teaching materials for history, social science, and linguistics, should be consistent with each other.

(C) The teaching of local languages, mathematics, social science, physics, chemistry, and natural science should, to the extent possible, be related to the important issues of socialist organization.

(D) Special emphasis should be placed on historical facts in social science, national language, literature, geography, and other subjects.

(E) Increase the teaching time for mathematics so that students can acquire sufficient knowledge in this training area to meet the needs of admission to higher education.

(F) In physics, Newton's laws should be explained in detail. In biology, the human body and the concept of cells should be developed. In addition, a more systematic chemistry curriculum should be established. When teaching geography, emphasis must be placed on knowledge of maps (especially knowledge of maps of the Soviet Union), as well as basic knowledge of topographic geography and economic geography. The geography of capitalist countries should also be included in the curriculum.

(G) At least one foreign language should be added in secondary schools.

(H) Improve the teaching methods for national language and social science.

(L) In the subjects of social science, literature, national language, geography, and history, the national culture of the people in the anti-Soviet Union and its literature, art, and science should be introduced.

(I) In vocational schools, emphasis should be placed on manual labor. In the teaching plan, the production work in industry should be integrated with theory.

In addition to the above, it is also necessary to have the elements of technological knowledge, for example, the minimum essential knowledge of electricity, the knowledge of the application of electricity in machinery and chemical industry. Furthermore, in order to gain practical knowledge, students must also visit electrical factories and must have the ability to use tools, wood, and metal to work.

Page 15

Free Talk

A Supplement to the Theory of Mutual Subjugation between "Writing" and "Teaching" 225

by Cao Juren

"Writing books is all for the sake of rice and grain, I worry about my frugal belly and lofty talk. In case I drift away in the sea of writing, people will ask where to sign my name without sorrow."

Cao Liwu collected Gong Ding'an's sentences

Teaching for ten years, no one does not shake their heads and sigh, hence Mr. Xia Yuanzun's saying "I would rather die early than be a teacher." Selling manuscripts for ten years, no one does not shake their heads and sigh, hence Mr. Zhuan Donghua's theory of "this road does not work." I have been teaching for thirteen years, and selling manuscripts for almost ten years. Exhausted, I have thoughts of returning home. Yesterday, I read Mr. Yu Dafu's "Writing Books and Teaching," which stirred my heart. I feel that his "theory of mutual subjugation between writing and teaching" comes from the bottom of his heart, and every sentence "first finds my heart." However, from the perspective of someone like me who has carried both burdens, the way of mutual subjugation does not lie in the professions of "writing" and "teaching" themselves, but outside of themselves.

"Writing" and "teaching" are close to the esteemed title of "freelancer." Is the profession really "free"? One must also ask the editor of "Free Talk" if the discussion is really "free." We are likely comrades: having the name of "free" but not the reality of "free." A writer, with accumulated ideas and experiences, wants to write a book, collecting materials for five years, organizing materials for two years, then grinding ink and unfolding paper, drafting for two years, and revising for one year, and then it is completed. Wouldn't that be great? A teacher, after years of research and creating new ideas, then ascends the stage to lecture, going from deep to shallow, encountering sources everywhere, making stubborn stones nod their heads and swimming fish look up. Wouldn't that be a joyous thing? Freelancers must often have such dreams, but what is the reality? The bookstore owner limits you to completing a 200,000-word book in three months. Feel free to copy and paste, no need to be original. The school owner asks you to teach for twenty-four hours a week, with seven or eight different courses, preparing on the spot and selling them immediately, with no stock left at home. The books written and taught by freelancers are nothing more than commodities on the market: the more you produce, the faster you produce, the more generous the boss, and only then can you make a "rice and grain." As for whether "inspiration" and "poetic sentiment" are permanently lost, that is not within the boss's calculations. Therefore, there are few times when "writing" and "teaching" mutually subjugate each other, and many times when "writing" and "teaching" are subjugated at the same time. Under the power of capitalism, the breath of freelancers is also too short!

In my experience, if you take teaching as the center of gravity for making a living and writing as a way to express your interests, then while teaching is certainly torturous, writing is relatively able to proceed gradually according to your own plans and complete a satisfactory work. Or, if you take writing as the center of gravity for making a living and teaching as a way to express your interests, teaching for only two or three hours a week, then when the inspiration strikes, the whole class can be silent and still, like eating ginseng fruit, with your whole body feeling comfortable. Or, change your plans and entrust the center of gravity for making a living to another profession, treating both "writing" and "teaching" as hobbies. Outside of selling manuscripts for稿費 and teaching for salary, there is room for free creation. Instead of mutually subjugating each other, they generate each other, and the achievements will surely be even more impressive. Mr. Zhou Zuoren said, "It is best for everyone not to take creation as a specialized career, but to have other skills and other professions besides creation. This will be even better for literature. If you rely solely on literature as a means of making a living, then if such people increase, it will inevitably lead to the depravity of literature." (The Origins and Development of Chinese New Literature) It can be seen that taking "writing" and "teaching" as a side business is another great way to preserve "inspiration" and "poetic sentiment."

John Stuart Mill worked as a clerk in the East India Company, serving for thirty years, and in his spare time, he wrote such a great masterpiece as Logic. Sometimes I want to learn how to repair cars, sometimes I want to learn to be a doctor, sometimes I want to learn to be a barber, and sometimes I even want to be a doorman for some great person, just hoping that I don't have to rely on the "writing" and "teaching" freelancing to make a living.

In conclusion, intellectuals have already reached the end of the road!

Killing the Goose to Get the Eggs 226

by Jingzi

A fellow villager came and said that the province is now levying a national salvation donation, totaling five million yuan, with each county being allocated tens of thousands to hundreds of thousands, and a deadline for payment. The so-called allocation is to allocate it to the general farmers according to the land tax. However, at present, every two acres of land tax in this province has additional taxes and donations reaching more than forty yuan, which means that the additional tax exceeds the regular tribute by more than ten times. Thinking of the huge number of "five million yuan," my heart feels inexplicably heavy. I don't know how many tragedies of selling children and daughters will be enacted under this number of five million. But if the donation is really for "saving the country," who can say that selling children and daughters is not necessary?

However, Hunan is perhaps slightly better than Sichuan.

According to the Sichuan Monthly Report compiled by the Bank of China: In March of this year, the 20th Army began to levy the grain tax for the 49th year, requiring it to be collected within 40 days; before the 21st year, the 24th Army levied four times a year. Last autumn, from the 36th year to the 38th year, it also levied a national defense donation of 25 yuan. From September to November, it also levied from the 30th year to the 41st year, and in December, it also levied from the 42nd year to the 44th year. In February of this year, it also levied the two years of the 45th and 46th years; the 28th Army stipulated that grain should be levied once every two months, that is, six years a year. Starting in March of this year, it also began to levy the grain tax for the 62nd and 63rd years and set a deadline for collection, with an additional levy for those who exceed the deadline, which is said to be "to warn the weary." Levying grain tax six times a year, and it is still only the 23rd year of the Republic of China, but the grain tax has already been levied to the 63rd year. I truly admire the spirit of the Chinese military in "killing the goose to get the golden eggs."

I heard that in the provinces of Shaanxi and Gansu, taxes and donations are used to exploit the people. Farmers who own land are even more miserable than general tenant farmers and hired laborers. Because the exploitation of taxes and donations for tenant farmers and hired laborers is relatively less, while general owner-farmers bear the name of "owning land" and are fundamentally unable to cope with the heavy taxes and donations. Therefore, they all lead their sons and daughters, posting the land deeds on the door, willingly wandering and drifting in all directions. The ancient poem "Sell new silk in February, sell new grain in May" is generally considered to be "healing the sore in front of the eyes, but cutting out the flesh of the heart." What about now? Now there is a chorus of selling children and daughters, and the tragedy of exchanging children for food is raging like a tiger. How can the people not be poor? How can the rural economy not become increasingly bankrupt?

The government is now loudly calling for rescuing the countryside, and some people even advocate that China should imitate the American method of rescuing the countryside. I think, instead of talking loftily about relief, the first step is still better to prohibit "killing the goose to get the eggs!"

Three Days 227

— Wu

The third day after the good day, the guests gradually dispersed.

I also went to the factory to work. I left the warm, soft new bed and the shy new bride early in the morning. I told her softly that I was going to work. She frowned and didn't say anything. I guessed she had something on her mind, reluctant to part, but I also felt she was annoyed with me, complaining about me. She hadn't said a word to me in three days. Was it shyness?: :

So I didn't say much more. I put on my usual work clothes

, put the leftover rice from last night into a box as usual, came out, and entrusted it to Sister Zhang downstairs, asking her to accompany the bride. She was new here, unfamiliar with everything, and also a bit lonely. Sister Zhang also smiled knowingly:

"Go ahead with peace of mind. No one will mistreat your bride.

Who would steal her away?"

"I'm just worried about you, afraid you'll steal her." As I

joked with her, I came out feeling light and refreshed, my heart warm and full of joy. The men and women going to work on the road were very crowded. I felt they were all smiling at me and teasing me. I am the happiest person in the world now. I am thirty-two years old this year, and I have been single since my father and mother passed away. How lonely these past ten years have been. But now I have a woman, and the loneliness and hardship of the past ten years have finally been rewarded. I am the happiest now: : And besides, the bride has such a fair, oval face, her eyes sparkling and charming, she is not bad looking at all.

I walked into the factory, and only today did I realize how

dark the factory was, how complicated the machines were, and how noisy the machine sounds were. I felt somewhat estranged from everything. When my colleagues saw me coming, they all asked questions, long and short, with smiling faces.

"Hey, how's the wife?"

"Original goods?"

"Happy, didn't sleep at night?"

"Reluctant to separate? Is the taste good?"

These kinds of interesting words fell on me like raindrops.

I actually became the center of attention among them. I am usually not paid much attention to. I am very grateful to them, so I greeted them cheerfully. That foreman also came over and patted me on the shoulder today, relaxing his stern face. The gentlemen walked by, heard others teasing me, and did not interfere, just smiled at me. How happy is this? A man with a wife is so respected.

I am thirty-two this year, and the woman is only twenty-one. I am eleven years older than her. As I worked, I heard someone saying in my ear: Now you have a family, and people respect you. You are eleven years older than the woman, you should cherish her and give her a good life. You have to work hard, you have to save more money, and soon you will have children. You have to work hard: : You are eleven years older than the woman: :

So I decided from today onwards to exert all my

strength, do the work of two people alone, and ask the gentlemen to give me double wages. When I go back after work in the evening, I will also look for something else to do.

How long the days in the factory are. Only today did I

realize how slowly time passes. As usual, it is twelve hours, but I thought a year had passed. I don't know how my bride is doing at home. I heard that she can cook and do everything herself. I thought about going back today, and someone has already cooked the meal and is waiting for me, how delicious that would be. I have a home now: It was not easy to wait until the factory blew the whistle for the end of work. I squeezed out of the crowd in a hurry. My heart was beating very fast along the way. I think this is because of happiness. My heart has lost its normal state.

Walking back to the workshop, the people in the alley all looked at me with strange

eyes, as if they wanted to search for something on me, staring at me from head to toe, confirming my back. Could something have happened to me, to my home? Someone should be cooking in my home and waiting for me.

At the door, I met Sister Zhang. As soon as she saw me,

she took my hand, seemingly trembling a little. Stepping through the front door, I said, "Where is she?"

"Her? I went out for half a day this afternoon. I just

came back and she was already gone."

"Gone. I searched everywhere, but there's no trace of her.

Someone saw her leaving with a bag of clothes. Go and see, the new room has been messed up. She ran away!"

Ran away. Is there such a thing? I ran up the stairs,

kicked open the door, and sure enough, I saw clothes scattered messily on the bed and on the floor, and the chest open. She no longer lives in the room. I felt my limbs go weak, and everything went dark before my eyes. I went to sit on a

chair, and the chair fell with my body. Now I am alone again, with no relatives to turn to, and I feel that I no longer have the courage to live.

Carrot Top 228

— Translated by JUUESKENARQ Lin Dao

Red Cheeks One (continued)

However, this time someone answered him:

"Yes, so what?"

Carrot Top shrunk back into the quilt.

Mr. Inspector appeared again, he appeared suddenly.

Two

"That's right," Wei Ao said, "I did kiss you, Maso;" You can admit this, because you did nothing wrong.

I kissed you on the forehead, but Carrot Top, who has fallen at a young age, cannot understand this. He does not know that this is a pure and innocent kiss, a kiss from a father to his son. He doesn't know that I love you as much as I love my own son. If you want, you can say like a brother. He will spread rumors everywhere tomorrow, this idiot! When Wei Ao Long said this, his voice trembled with anger, but Carrot Top pretended to be asleep. But he still perked up his head to listen.

Masao held his breath and listened to the inspector's words. Although he felt that his words were very natural, he trembled all over, as if fearing some mysterious revelation. Wei Ao Long continued, trying to keep his voice down. These were some vague words, some fleeting syllables. Carrot Top, who was lying in bed and dared not turn over, moved his waist slightly and unconsciously came closer. At this time, he couldn't hear anything. His attention was excited to the extreme. He felt that his two ears had indeed become two holes, and that the holes had expanded to become like funnels: but no sound fell into these funnels.

He remembered the same feeling of effort he often had when eavesdropping outside the door. At that time, while listening, he leaned his eyes on the keyhole to peek, wishing he could enlarge the keyhole and pull the things he wanted to steal closer to see clearly, as if hooking them with an iron hook. But at this time, he really heard Wei Ao Long say again:

"Yes, my love is pure, pure, and that's what that idiot can't understand!"

Finally, the inspector bent down with a shadow-like tenderness and kissed Maso on the forehead. The mustache under his chin stroked Maso's forehead like a writing brush. Then he straightened up and walked outside. Carrot Top followed him closely with his eyes, watching him pass between the rows of beds. When Wei Ao Long's hand touched someone else's pillow, the awakened person sighed heavily and turned over to the other side. (To be continued)

, the market has gradually become prosperous, the cocoon quality is also excellent, and the price is also expected to be high. Improved high-quality cocoons open at 34-35 to 37-38 yuan, and ordinary ones are pulled at 30 yuan.

Chang'an 254

Cocoon houses have been open for three days. The goods arrived on the first day were not good, and the cocoon price only opened at 26-27 yuan. In the past two days, more improved high-quality cocoons have arrived, and the cocoon price has risen from 3

14-15 yuan to 37-38 yuan.

Zhejiang 255

The Department of Construction designated Xiaoshan and Lin'an counties as model first and second improved sericulture areas this year, distributing improved seeds and dispatching instructors to guide breeding. The silkworm season is particularly

good, and new cocoons are being launched one after another, with excellent results. A special call was made to the financial community

Silk cocoon merchants form a cocoon collection committee, with six committee members recommended in each district, raising huge sums of money (100,000 in Xiaoshan and 60,000 in Lin'an) to rent cocoon houses and collect cocoons in each district. It is reported that the two model areas are expected to collect 45,000 to 46,000 dan of fresh cocoons this year. They have all set off separately.

Discussions

Telegrams or Cannons? 260

— Tianfang

In this year of great turmoil, seeing the domestic situation and the regressive state of affairs, one cannot help but laugh and cry. No, only anger!

The four northeastern provinces have been lost and have not yet been recovered, and Peiping and Tianjin are also in danger. All those who have the blood of the Yellow Emperor flowing in their veins and who have the nationality of the "Republic of China" should unite and rise up to save themselves. However, the facts tell us the opposite.

The national crisis has been going on for two years. During these two years, the suffering of the 30 to 40 million people in the three northeastern provinces under the iron hooves of foreign races is unimaginable. Even the people of the whole country, due to the intensification of the imperialist policy of aggression, have led to the collapse of the countryside and the bankruptcy of the national economy. Among the 474 million people, except for a few high-ranking Chinese officials who can still leisurely enjoy themselves in dance halls and theaters, the rest have been plunged into an abyss.

However, the sound of the cannons of the imperialists cannot awaken the dreams of the intoxicated people, nor can it change the minds of the warlords. In these two years since the outbreak of the national crisis, we have seen a lot of news about the war. In addition to the loyal and courageous resistance of the Northeast Volunteer Army and the 19th Route Army, we have also heard of the infighting of the two Chens in Guangdong, the conflicts between Han and Liu in Shandong, the uncle and nephew fighting of Liu Xiang and Liu Wenhui in Sichuan, and the internal strife in Guizhou, Xinjiang, and Tibet. We really cannot use an abacus to calculate the lives and property sacrificed under these topics. All the compatriots who participated in these wars, after crying and fleeing, must say "serves them right" when they think of the people they usually raised who gave them pain!

We know that the invasion and massacre of foreign races is to destroy our country, but are the warlords'肆行 wars and署杀 going to destroy our nation? The warlords must be very clear about this, but we "A Dou" who are drunk and dreaming, are still ignorant, and exhaust our fat to raise executioners to massacre ourselves.

The civets raised in our homes are easily satisfied in their desires, and they can also catch rats and guard the house, doing their best for their masters. The warlords are not like this. The fatter you raise them, the more you want them to be safe, the more pain they will give you. In Sichuan, which is known as a rich area in the country, isn't the land tax already pre-collected until the 60th year of the Republic of China? The taxes of the era of our children and grandchildren have all been paid. These obedient people can be said to be "obedient" to the extreme. In theory, they should have peace and enjoy their remaining years. However, the equivalent price paid is the practice of 478 wars in 20 years, and they have suffered all the misery of exile.

Recently, the warlords Liu Wenhui and Deng Xihou of Sichuan Province have once again started a war because of "conflicts of interest," creating the record of the 479th civil war in Sichuan Province. According to reports, this war has extended to 800 Chinese miles and mobilized 400,000 people. Its scale is far greater than that of the isolated resistance of Su Ma, Li Du, and the 19th Route Army, which received no support. It is worth writing about in the future history of the Republic of China. When it comes to foreign affairs, they say "lack of military supplies" and "inconvenient transportation," but when it comes to internal affairs, new weapons are readily available. This kind of elusive military ingenuity, with various tricks, what else can we "A Dou" say besides admiration.

Whenever a civil war occurs, as usual, all parties will send out many telegrams, "imploring" and ordering. But as usual, it is not until one party is defeated that someone comes out to accept what is called "imploring" and "ordering." It is the cannons that win, but the general "A Dou" are sacrificed between this acceptance and non-acceptance. As for the result of the war, "the winner is king," and the name is naturally "punishing the rebels." What about the defeated side? Just like the lesson of the elder Mr. Yuan, he cupped his hands and said, "See you in five years." So five years, or not even five years later, justice turned again, and the second "punishment of the rebels" began, and so on to the third, fourth, four hundred and seventy-ninth, and so on. And the like of "A Dou" will always breathe between the cracks of people's interests.

Telegrams have become the only remedy for saving the country and dealing with all things. This time is no exception. There are telegram appeals from 70 million people in Sichuan and orders from the Executive Yuan to stop it, but the facts tell us that these appeal telegrams are like shouting "God save me." No matter how tearfully you speak, it will never move the heart of the murdering devil. Then, the only effective way to protect our lives and property, "a change of mind can achieve it" (original text of the Sichuan people's good telegram), is:

Rise up and no longer raise any domestic thieves!

Page 18

Brief Thoughts After Reading the "Shen Bao Yearbook" 261

— Shibben

After the publication of the "Shen Bao Yearbook," because of its rich content

'All materials relating to party affairs, politics, military affairs, economy, education, transportation, society, academics, industry, etc. have been collected, and the compilation is novel', classified, precise and detailed, so within a few days of its release, it has become popular at home and abroad. The one I'm talking about', was just mailed to me by the post office yesterday', although I just flipped through it hastily', it has already sparked a lot of thoughts', I'll write a few of them below:

Among the resolutions of the Fourth National Congress',

there is a proposal by Liu Jiashu and 43 others: "Strictly order officials in all provinces to strictly guard the territory and not abandon their duties"-what effect does this kind of resolution have? Don't you see that General Tang of Rehe has already violated this resolution' and retreated without fighting, abandoning the defense', losing the entire province of Rehe, the shield of North China', causing the current crisis in Peiping and Tianjin? Tang Yulin's sins are profound, but it can be seen that the senior officials of the country's borders' cannot strictly abide by and implement the resolutions of the highest authority's congress', so everything else is needless to say.

Seeing He Ruqun and 28 others' proposal: "The case of earnestly protecting overseas Chinese"', I remembered that in recent days', the overseas Chinese in Mexico' have been expelled one after another', more than 4,000 people' according to the refugee representatives: there are still more than 10,000 large numbers of overseas Chinese' who will also be deported back home soon', alas! The treatment of overseas Chinese in a country', whether they can live and work in the country of residence', depends on the strength of their home country's international status', our noble country' is plagued by internal and external troubles', and the country is about to perish', of course it will be despised', abused', expelled', and arbitrarily treated'. The "case of earnestly protecting overseas Chinese" in a weak country's diplomacy' is naturally an unfulfilled check'! Reading "General Situation of the Army"', I know that our noble country is indeed the country with the most armies in the world'. Its number' is really alarming', with more than 2 million', alas! With so many troops', and the Japanese devils invaded', except for the 19th Route Army and Song Zheyuan and other minority troops, no one was willing to defend the country and resist the enemy', allowing the arrogant dogs to rush around', as if entering no man's land', killing people everywhere! Mountains and rivers change color'! Alas! Raising soldiers for a thousand days', using them for a day', with such an army' that I compare to "every bush and tree looks like an enemy soldier"', but in the end no one went to kill the enemy and resist', then all the soldiers are "all grass and trees"'.

China's air force' is also increasingly ashamed'. Even the airline's commercial planes' and the people's "Fords" and "Sykes" are all counted, and there are only 274 planes in the whole of China'. Compared with the thousands of planes in other countries', it is really a small sight to see a big one'. Therefore, patriots advocate that saving the country must first expand the air force'. As a result, various places have started raising money to purchase planes' to implement "aviation to save the country"'. But I think that with planes', but continuing the old habits of "non-resistance" and adhering to the "calm" effort', then even if there are as many as thousands or hundreds of planes', they will still be useless'. Don't you see that the "Shen Bao Yearbook" says' that Zhang Xueliang had 500 planes in the Northeast', but because of the three words "non-resistance"', all of them were looted as enemy spoils'. Therefore, "non-resistance" will not be defeated one day', it is better to buy one less plane', saving it for the enemy to create wealth'.

Yesterday's newspaper reported that the newly appointed Chairman of the Peiping Political Affairs

If I Had a Child 263

— Cun Xin

If I had a child, how would I teach and raise him? I often wonder.

Firstly, I know that an ideal child should have an ideal mother to nurture him. This ideal mother doesn't need to be worldly wise, but it doesn't hurt if she's a little naive. She should at least know a bit about art and be able to tell a few stories. Because children's hearts are light and beautiful, they need a beautiful environment to adapt to. When the child is sleeping in the cradle, the ideal mother should often play some organ music or similar things for him to listen to. Because there is no beauty more intangible than music, and it is also what children can best perceive. As for the placement of the child's bed, there should naturally be a beautiful and lively environment nearby. In the room, if there aren't any real flowers, some paper flowers should also be prepared. On the walls, instead of hanging some profound landscape paintings, it's better to hang some colorful watercolor paintings. But when the child grows up, among the watercolor paintings that he's tired of looking at, you must insert some photos of great people (including revolutionaries, scientists, thinkers, writers, artists, etc., but not important officials of the party and the country) so that they can gain inspiration in life from these fresh materials. If he cries, which is common for children, you must check the source of this reaction. Is it lack of milk? Or is it cold or hot? Let me tell you, never hold him out of indulgence, because all of a child's actions have no predetermined goal, and it's all trial and error. If the trial is wrong, he will correct it himself, and you must not give him bad suggestions. Furthermore, if he can walk and is tired of playing with clay dolls, you can teach him to get close to kittens, puppies, chicks, ducklings, and the like. This can allow him to come into contact with external things and cultivate his loving empathy, and it's definitely not just appreciating the small voices, the yellow feathers, and the exquisite postures. If he has a need for knowledge, then the ideal mother should often tell him some stories. The stories should be beautiful, but even absurd stories have a limit. The travels of chicks and ducklings and the fights of kittens and puppies are also fine, because he will eventually be able to verify that it's just a story. But if you tell him about gods, then this delusion will be difficult for him to eradicate forever. And don't tell ugly things, such as ghosts and monsters, which will hurt their beautiful hearts. In short, all these skills are things that every ideal mother should be familiar with and don't need to be explained in detail. Furthermore, if he gets carried away playing for a while and breaks your beloved clock or other objects, then you shouldn't be angry and punish him. You must know that this is the beginning of creation, and you should help him fix it. Things in the world cannot be accomplished at once. You must not use your adult-stage experience to reprimand inexperienced children. Negative reprimands are not as good as positive encouragement. Your responsibility is to increase children's interest in learning. What must also be remembered is that when children are playing their symbolic games, you must not destroy the houses they draw on the ground or trample on the imaginary characters. This is also a kind of cruelty that is enough to hurt their beautiful hearts. And when you are working, such as planting flowers and raising pigeons, you can ask your children to help. For them, this is sure to be readily obeyed, and they can also learn a little common sense, which they will definitely find more interesting than attending a nature class. The most important thing is to make children feel that doing things is a game, not dull drudgery.

Finally, we must know that the purpose of educating children is to make them have an independent personality and skills to deal with the world, and the parents' responsibilities are limited to the completion of the above two tasks. So I often think, if I had money and could afford a means of transportation, I would never want my son to go to school in a chartered car, but would buy him a bicycle and let him bump his nose and eyes together and break his hands and feet into eight pieces. I believe that one more failure will definitely lead to one more success. The responsibility of parents is to guide their children onto the road to independence, and definitely not to be 'oxen and horses' for life.

I would like to offer my opinions to men and women who are already or will become fathers and mothers.

Six-Character Marriage Proposal 264

— Zhi Kuan

The previous issue of this magazine had a six-character joke. Yesterday, while I was free at home, I casually read the newspapers and magazines and suddenly discovered a marriage proposal advertisement. The words were also in six-character phrases. It was truly a rare coincidence. After reading it, I specially extracted the original text and submitted it to this magazine. Readers, please do not ridicule it as a clumsy imitation.

This little one is twenty-eight, still waiting for a husband in her boudoir,

Though my figure isn't gorgeous, my attire is quite modern,

The purpose of life after marriage is to be with you day and night,

Travel with a car, live in a three-story Western-style house,

Eat at the same table, walk hand in hand when going out,

Dancing is being practiced, gambling skills are already all mastered,

If you enjoy this way, I guarantee you will be satisfied,

If you agree with the marriage proposal terms, you can first communicate secretly,

If both parties are satisfied, you can freely get engaged,

If the relationship is deep, you can open the shop later, transactions can also be carried out first,

If there are disagreements later, divorce is absolutely free,

Garret Room 265

— Yan Meng

Needing rest, thinking of stillness after extreme activity, this is originally human nature. If one believes in fate because of not having better opportunities, that is going backwards beyond reason. The economy is in recession, society is becoming increasingly fragmented, and the national crisis is even more severe. The giant wheels of the times are constantly turning, and everything is being swept into the wheels.

Rely on one's own strength to build one's own world,

Without relying on any external assistance, then what else do we displaced people have besides living in garret rooms? Complaining is useless and foolish. Friends, quickly seek our new world.

However, revolutionary theories, philosophies of love,

And great art are not nurtured in high-rise buildings but are budding in garret rooms. Poets, thinkers, literary giants... they all hide in garret rooms, pushing forward their own time, and each will is always throwing their youth in small sorrows, bitter faces, or cheerful conversations!

Page 19

Garret room, as the name suggests, should be a beautiful

"pavilion on the water"? But who knows that it is specifically carrying the disappointed, the unemployed, the exiles, burying the young people with great ambitions but no food? In such a country, in such a tragic and bleak phenomenon, if the Chinese youth are not so ignorant and numb, and good at comforting themselves, at least a large part of them would have committed suicide.

The weather is gradually getting hot, and I, who am used to living in garret

rooms, have lived in Chinese, semi-Chinese, semi-Western, and Western-style garret rooms. Now I have moved to a garret room in the French Concession. Every day, I go out early and return late to carry out our business. What do I care about the splendor or shabbiness of the room?

Novel

The Life of Wu Ji (Sixteenth Installment) 268

— Ling He

"No matter who comes today, tell them I'm not home."

"Then what about young master Zhang? Is he also not allowed in?"

"You blockhead, didn't I call him to come? Of course, you can lead him straight to my room."

Soon, she fell asleep again. This time, she slept for a long time, until a faint yellow dusk appeared at the windows. When she woke up for the second time, she saw that Zhang Wenbin was already sitting in front of her bed.

"Oh, when did you come? Why didn't you wake me up?" she said happily.

"Miss, I didn't dare to disturb you. You were too tired."

"But didn't you wait too long? Aren't you complaining at all?"

"Miss, you know I am very content. I watched you sleeping quietly, your gentle breathing, your beautiful languid state, to the point that even the sweet and soft air in this room can make me boast of my happiness. So what's there to be unsatisfied about? Would I want to be jealous of my own happiness?"

"Child!" She suddenly held his hand. "I didn't expect you to be so eloquent. You know that it's easy to win a woman's heart like this."

"Then how do you plan to love your lovely child?"

"What else do you want from me? Aren't you already sitting by my bed?"

At this time, Zhang Wenbin really became bold and kissed her hand tightly. It was a mysterious force that excited her to the point that she wanted to hold his head and kiss his lips passionately, but she still heavily stopped herself.

Movie Special

Movie Stars at Middle Age 269

— Zhong Qin

Those Who Aren't Blessed with Enduring Beauty Risk Being Abandoned, Leaving the Scene by Traveling

In Hollywood's movie scene, new stars spring up like mushrooms after rain, one after another, jumping onto the screen without any sign of stopping. At the same time, many stars who are past middle age gradually lose their luster in batches. Those older stars who are content retire and rest, or go traveling. Those who are not content gradually have no one to support them, their star power disappears, and they gradually fail and decline. This phenomenon is ceaseless in Hollywood. Metabolism is of course an unavoidable process for anything in the world, but this phenomenon of the old and the new replacing each other is even more pronounced in the movie city of Hollywood.

Some people say that Hollywood's movie scene is like a political stage, with changes that are impossible to predict. This is indeed a precise analogy. In Hollywood, actresses rely on their youth to gain a position in Hollywood. It's already very difficult to maintain that position for more than five years. As for a red-hot star, it's impossible to remain red for many years. How many stars in Hollywood stay in the movie industry for ten years? Once their youth passes, their opportunities in Hollywood also diminish. By middle age, it's impossible to stay in Hollywood any longer. Even if there are a few, like Mary Pickford, who recently still starred in a United Artists film called "Secrets" in Hollywood, half of it was relying on her past fame, and the other half was relying on good makeup techniques to make people in Hollywood unable to tell that she was already a middle-aged woman. Furthermore, this "Secrets" was actually filmed several years ago. As for whether she is willing to work in the future, it is still unknown. To give another example, when Pola Negri was first crowned as the queen of Hollywood movies, how glorious she was. Now, however, she is no longer able to obtain her former glory. The film "The Woman from Moscow", which was recently shown in Shanghai, is undoubtedly her last work.

As for saying that Marie Dressler was an old woman, how could she be the queen of Hollywood? Marie Dressler is indeed the only one in Hollywood history who can be considered an exception. Moreover, although she was also made a queen, she played old characters. The older and uglier she was, the better. She cannot be compared with many stars who rely solely on their youth to make money. Actresses in Hollywood are extremely terrified of the arrival of middle age. Their only way to avoid showing their middle age is makeup, but artificiality is ultimately false. Therefore, when they reach middle age, they are still eliminated one by one and cannot escape. Resting and long-distance travel are just a facade for their departure. The vicissitudes of life are also a natural trend.

Film Review

Re-review of "Career" 270

— Ming

Indeed, the first failure of this film lies in the weak consciousness of the script. We can see that the people in the first act have very contradictory actions and thoughts before and after (as told by the subtitles). The sudden changes make people feel that some of the people in the film are similar to fiction and have no unified personality. This is already enough to make the plot extremely scattered, let alone explain the central meaning clearly? The so-called "career path for women" is just a female performer returning to her old profession? It does not indicate a bright path. I am not saying that acting is not a profession, but most people must admit that being a performer is not a long-term profession. When youth fades and skills decline, one will be eliminated. So is a woman's career only temporary?

Moreover, the screenwriter seems to oppose love and marriage. Once there is a rift between husband and wife, they should separate and never allow reconciliation after repentance. This point may not be permitted by reason. It is true that a man can interact with many women at the same time, but a woman cannot talk with anyone other than her husband. Indeed, this is a distorted phenomenon in society, so the screenwriter also seems not to give the "official person" who does not allow his wife to have affairs and impose excessive punishment on her and does not allow him to repent, because he does not know that his wife sacrificed for him, so he turned his face completely. This is something understandable.

The director is also too negligent. For the scenery and so on, he only tries his best to seek their splendor and does not think about whether reality should be like this. The control of the actors is also very inappropriate. In small places, there are loopholes to be found. The photography is good, and the movement of the camera is also very lively, but the close-ups reflected by the mirror are used too much, which makes people tired. Star Film Company has the best light in domestic films, and this time it also maintains its past achievements. Although Xuan Jinglin is inevitably somewhat "past her prime", her performance is still good. There are some new dramatic elements in many places, and the director and actors should be responsible for this. Sun Min is too cautious, so she is too rigid. Wang Jiting can tell at a glance that he is playing a gangster, but he also has some merit in portraying a general playboy-style philistine. Zhu Qiuheng's performance is too over the top, completely losing the identity of a female secretary.

The subtitles are relatively good, concise and meaningful, and the scene division is not chaotic.

Ruan Lingyu's Wonderful Words 271

A part of the staff of Lianhua No. 2 Factory was filming the exterior scenes of "Little Toys" in Wuxi and lived in the Rong family villa. There were more mosquitoes and insects here than in Shanghai, so most people couldn't sleep well at night. One morning, Wan Lingyu got up early and took a walk in front of the flowers. She met Sun Yu. Sun asked, "Miss Ruan, did you sleep well last night?" Ruan frowned and said with a charming smile: "I didn't sleep well! The mosquitoes are too annoying. I think, when will our Chinese mosquitoes all become airplanes? Then China will be strong."

Audience Opinions

"Career" Gives Us Understanding 272

— Feng Ying

Undoubtedly, in the present era when women's rights have reached a surging period, various occupations in society are gradually having opportunities for women to get involved. The feudal phenomenon of "relying on men for a living" in the past has been eliminated by the times and will gradually diminish. However, in the transition between this old and new process, there are still many women who "rely on men for a living," and of course, men who play with women have not been completely eliminated.

This time, the star "Career" that is showing at the Central is very clearly intended to awaken women who "rely on men for a living" and are played with by men, and to indicate their way out: self-reliance is indeed a great inspiration for women of the times, and it is worth our attention.

In the plot, Junjie's unrestrained and dissolute behavior with his female secretary in the office after becoming an official, I think this kind of description of a licentious rogue is probably a strange phenomenon that truly high-ranking officials may not have. In the last scene when Lan Ying was about to leave, Junjie used the sentence "What will women do without men?" to attack the weakness of women who "rely on men for a living," but Lan Ying had a skill, gave up that life of being played with by men, and went to seek her own independent career path.

Zhang Shichuan's directing skills have indeed improved a lot compared to before. He is unwilling to relax at all in terms of the plot. This film is not his success.

In terms of actors, we have not seen Xuan Jinglin for a long time. This time on the screen, she tells us that her art is indeed good. Sun Min and Zhu Qiuheng's expressions are very realistic. What about the rest?

In short, the film tightly grasps the weakness of a part of women in society who "rely on men for a living" and issues a warning. At the same time, it gives a strong warning to men who use women as toys.

"Career" Is a Guide to Women's Way Out 273

— Yu Jiaqing

In every film, its title carries artistic meaning, such as the recent "New Year's Eve," "Awakening," "Women's Cry," and "Morning in the City," etc. "Career" is also one of them. Its advertisement has been promoted for a long time in the newspapers. Today is its first public screening at the Central Grand Theater. In order to try the film's art, I took a special trip to admire it.

The plot of this film tells us that relying on men is not beneficial. It also tells us that women must have a spirit of independence and the ability to save themselves, otherwise it will make you "self-harm." The plot is desirable, realistic, and novel. It guides the way out for modern women.

The director does not have any amazing good points in this film. It is somewhat more progressive than in "Broken Love" and more backward than in "Rouge Market." There are no skills, and there are many loopholes.

None of the actors have moving performances. Xuan Jinglin's performance is much worse than in "A Married Woman" at Dayi. Sun Min has made progress compared to "Rouge Market." The rest of the actors are just average.

After Watching "Career" 274

— Shi Zeyong

Since the release of "Women's Cry" by Star Film Company, the criticisms in the media have been consistently praised. And the recent films released are all very insightful and explanatory on women's issues. Of course, this obvious progress is indeed worthy of our admiration.

But today's release of "Career" at the Central has made people feel somewhat disappointed. Although this is another masterpiece by Mr. Ding Qianping after "Rouge Market," I dare not completely agree with and endorse it.

"Career," especially a woman's "career," is such a moving word and a matter that deserves attention! In this film, it inspires many women to recognize their own "career." It means that after a woman marries a husband, she should not be completely immersed in the river of love and rely on her husband. She must continue to work hard for her own "career." As in this film, the protagonist, Su Lan Ying, is a popular female performer. She abandons her stage life for marrying her husband, which is not her career at all. And her husband is an unfaithful overseas student. Once he is successful and becomes a director, he immediately changes his true colors, likes the new and tires of the old, and has another love. He even wants to insult and beat her. So Lan Ying suddenly realizes that she is unwilling to be insulted by a man. For the sake of her own personality and for the sake of her own "career," she still goes back to her original stage career. This is the destination of her career.

In summary, the consciousness of this "Career" makes me somewhat disappointed and not completely satisfied, because it does not provide a practical indication and explanation of what a career is. Compared with "Rouge Market," it is obviously a step backward.

Regarding the expressions of the actors, Xuan Jinglin, who plays Su Lan Ying, is the most suitable. Sun Min is obviously more advanced than in "Rouge Market"! Wang Jiheng is famous for his villain roles, and he is quite successful in this film. Gu Lanjun's performance is the most natural, but unfortunately, she appears too few times. In addition, the director's skills, the actors' expressions, and other photography scenery, etc., are worth watching.

The Eternal Regret of the Film Novel (THE WHITE SISTER) VIII 275

— Si Ping

He was gone. The beauty and joy of that sweet night were gone with him. But a kind of consciousness remained in her mind, comforting her. They are two lovers, that must be right. Trying to regain her composure, she followed her father back to the dance hall. Ernesto was annoyed because she had left, and Angela danced a waltz with him in his stubborn arms.

After the grand meeting, when the night was quiet, her father summoned her to his room. She went to him still wearing her evening dress. As soon as she met her father, she expressed her apologies. Prince Sheremetev realized that this matter could not be settled with an apology, and even heard Angela's tone implying that she regretted the marriage with Ernesto, which greatly alarmed him. She shouldn't break the engagement!

The conversation became more and more unpleasant. She openly said that she had fallen in love with that young soldier and that the soldier also loved her. Prince Sheremetev took out a rolled-up piece of paper from the drawer of his desk and said coldly that that was her marriage contract.

"Father!" Angela pleaded earnestly, "I originally wanted to do what you wanted me to do. I secretly prayed that I would love Ernesto, but I fell in love with Giovanni!"

"Love!" Her father's face became very ugly. "I'll tell you what love is! Do you know your mother? Do you recognize her?" He continued like a wild beast. "She ran away! With another man! Abandoned me! Do you understand!? Also because of love! She also thought she could find happiness! Oh, Angela, my child, believe me, I know which way is best for you: I want you to be happy, safe, and comfortable!"

"Where is mother now?" Angela asked, ignoring his pleas.

"She's dead." Prince Sheremetev, seeing that his heartfelt pleas could not make her change her mind, said angrily, "That man also abandoned her, so she committed suicide. That's your example! A soldier! Without a penny! You picked him up on the street!"

Angela defended Giovanni for a while and then sobbed and cried. She must go to see Giovanni, she can't not see him, she would rather die. She wailed and ran out of the room. (To be continued)
